General Liability Claim Reporting and Initial Duties
THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.

The provisions contained within this section establish the mandatory administrative procedures following any incident that may invoke coverage under this contract.

Strict adherence to these reporting protocols serves as a fundamental condition precedent to the availability of any liability protection provided herein.

You must implement internal organizational procedures to ensure that your management personnel are promptly made aware of any potential liability events.

Upon becoming aware of an event that could reasonably result in a liability demand, written notification must be transmitted to our claims department.

This initial notification must be dispatched as soon as practicable, regardless of whether a formal demand for compensation has been received.

The written incident report must include specific details regarding the time, date, and physical location where the unexpected event occurred.

You must also provide a comprehensive description of the circumstances surrounding the event, including the nature of the activities being performed.

The names, addresses, and contact information of any injured parties must be documented and submitted alongside the initial incident report.

If any witnesses were present during the event, their identifying information and contact details must also be secured and forwarded to us.

In the event that a formal legal demand or lawsuit is initiated against your organization, immediate notification is strictly required.

You must immediately record the date and time of receipt for any legal summons, complaint, or formal demand letter delivered to you.

All corresponding legal documents, correspondence, and related materials must be forwarded to our designated claims administration office without any delay.

Under no circumstances should you or any of your representatives voluntarily make any financial payments or assume any legal obligations.

Any voluntary assumption of liability or independent settlement offers made without our prior written consent will not be reimbursed under this contract.

You are strictly prohibited from incurring any independent expenses related to the incident, other than for immediate first aid at the scene.

The preservation of physical evidence related to the incident is a critical responsibility that falls entirely upon your organization.

You must take all reasonable steps to secure the incident scene and prevent any spoliation or alteration of relevant physical materials.

Photographic or video documentation of the incident location should be captured immediately, provided it is safe and legally permissible to do so.

Any equipment, machinery, or products involved in the event must be segregated and maintained in their immediate post-incident condition.

Failure to preserve critical evidence may severely prejudice the investigation and could result in the forfeiture of available liability protection.

If the incident involves potential criminal activity, such as theft or vandalism, you must promptly notify the appropriate local law enforcement authorities.

A copy of the official police report must be obtained and submitted to our claims department as part of your reporting obligations.

You must establish a centralized point of contact within your organization to facilitate all communications with our assigned claims professionals.

This designated representative must possess the authority to access necessary records and coordinate internal responses to our investigative inquiries.

All subsequent developments related to the reported incident must be communicated to our office in a timely and transparent manner.

You must not engage in any independent discussions regarding liability or settlement with the claimant or their legal representatives.

Any inquiries received from third-party investigators, media personnel, or opposing counsel must be immediately directed to our claims administration team.

Compliance with these reporting duties does not automatically guarantee that the reported event falls within the scope of available liability protection.

We reserve the authority to evaluate all submitted information to determine the applicability of specific coverage parts, exclusions, and limitations.

Your failure to fulfill these initial reporting obligations may result in a formal declination of coverage for the specific incident in question.

GL-CR-100Juniper Gate Learning Center, LLC | LG695378
Juniper Crown Casualty
Commercial General Liability
POLICY NUMBER: LG695378
EFFECTIVE: 04/01/2026
EXPIRES: 04/01/2027
Litigation Management and Defense Administration
THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.

1. Our organization assumes the exclusive authority to manage the legal response to any qualified liability demand presented against your enterprise.

This authority encompasses the complete direction of all litigation strategies, settlement negotiations, and the selection of appropriate legal representation.

When a qualified legal action is initiated, we will appoint legal counsel to represent your interests in the pending judicial proceedings.

The selection of the defense attorney remains entirely within our discretion, utilizing our network of approved legal professionals and specialized firms.

2. You may request the appointment of specific counsel; however, we are under no obligation to honor such requests unless mandated by jurisdiction.

The appointed legal counsel will focus solely on defending the allegations that fall within the scope of this commercial liability contract.

We maintain the authority to investigate any claim or suit at our discretion, utilizing internal personnel or independent investigative resources.

During the course of the litigation, we will determine the most appropriate legal strategy to mitigate potential financial exposures.

3. We possess the unilateral authority to negotiate and finalize the settlement of any claim or suit without requiring your explicit consent.

Our settlement decisions are based on a comprehensive evaluation of liability exposure, anticipated litigation costs, and jurisdictional venue factors.

If we determine that a negotiated resolution is the most prudent course of action, we will execute the settlement on your behalf.

Our obligation to provide legal representation ceases immediately upon the exhaustion of the applicable limit scheduled in the policy declarations.

4. Once the relevant limit has been entirely depleted through the payment of judgments or settlements, we will withdraw from the defense.

You will be formally notified in writing when the applicable limit is approaching exhaustion and when it has been fully depleted.

Following the depletion of the limit, the responsibility for funding any ongoing legal representation transfers entirely to your organization.

In situations where a lawsuit contains both covered allegations and allegations excluded by this contract, we will provide a defense for the entire action.

5. However, we reserve the right to issue a formal reservation of rights regarding the specific allegations that fall outside the coverage scope.

This reservation of rights ensures that our provision of a defense does not constitute a waiver of our right to deny financial responsibility.

We will not provide financial reimbursement for any judgments or settlements associated with the uncovered portions of the legal action.

You retain the option to hire independent legal counsel, at your own expense, to monitor the litigation and advise you on uncovered exposures.

6. Any independent counsel retained by your organization must fully cooperate with the primary defense attorney appointed by our claims department.

The primary defense attorney retains ultimate control over the direction of the litigation and the presentation of the defense in court.

We will not reimburse any legal fees, consultation costs, or administrative expenses incurred by your independently retained legal counsel.

If a conflict of interest arises that legally requires the appointment of independent defense counsel, we will fund such representation at prevailing rates.

7. The prevailing rates for independent counsel will be determined based on standard legal fees for similar litigation within the specific geographic venue.

We require the independent counsel to adhere to our standard litigation management guidelines and billing protocols throughout the duration of the case.

Any failure by the independent counsel to comply with these administrative guidelines may result in the reduction or denial of fee reimbursements.

The administration of the defense process is designed to protect both your organizational assets and our financial interests under this contract.

8. We will keep your designated organizational representative reasonably informed regarding significant developments and major strategic decisions during the litigation process.

Ultimately, the final determination regarding trial progression versus settlement resolution rests exclusively with our claims administration personnel.

GL-LM-200Juniper Gate Learning Center, LLC | LG695378
Juniper Crown Casualty
Commercial General Liability
POLICY NUMBER: LG695378
EFFECTIVE: 04/01/2026
EXPIRES: 04/01/2027
Investigation Assistance and Insured Cooperation Conditions
THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.

A. Your active and transparent participation in the fact-finding process is a mandatory requirement for the continuation of any liability protection.

The administrative framework of this contract relies upon your full cooperation to accurately assess the circumstances surrounding any reported incident.

When requested by our claims personnel, you must promptly provide access to all relevant organizational records, documents, and electronic data.

This includes, but is not limited to, employee training logs, maintenance schedules, operational manuals, and internal incident investigation reports.

You must facilitate interviews between our investigators and any of your employees, contractors, or agents who may possess relevant knowledge.

B. These interviews may be conducted in person, via telephone, or through virtual platforms, depending on the logistical requirements of the investigation.

If we deem it necessary, you and your employees must submit to formal examinations under oath regarding the details of the incident.

These examinations under oath will be recorded, and you may be required to sign a transcript verifying the accuracy of your statements.

You must assist our representatives in securing physical evidence and identifying third-party witnesses who can corroborate your version of events.

When requested, you must grant our investigators and retained experts unrestricted access to the physical premises where the incident occurred.

C. This access is necessary to conduct site inspections, take precise measurements, and perform forensic evaluations of the incident location.

During the course of any formal legal proceedings, your ongoing cooperation remains a critical condition of the provided defense services.

You must attend all required legal hearings, depositions, mediation sessions, and trial proceedings as directed by the appointed defense counsel.

Your organization must ensure that key personnel are available to testify truthfully and accurately regarding the facts of the case.

We will reimburse your organization for reasonable travel expenses and lost earnings incurred directly as a result of attending these required proceedings.

D. The maximum daily reimbursement rate for lost earnings is strictly capped at the amount specified in the administrative schedules.

You are expressly prohibited from taking any actions that might prejudice our ability to defend the claim or negotiate a favorable settlement.

Any intentional misrepresentation of facts, concealment of evidence, or collusion with the claimant will result in the immediate forfeiture of protection.

You must not enter into any agreements with third parties that attempt to assign liability or alter the legal dynamics of the claim.

If you possess any contractual rights to seek indemnification or financial recovery from another entity, you must preserve those rights entirely.

E. You are required to assist us in enforcing any such recovery rights against third parties who may be responsible for the incident.

This includes providing necessary documentation and testimony to support subrogation actions initiated by our legal recovery department.

Any financial recovery obtained from third parties will be distributed according to the specific recovery provisions outlined elsewhere in this contract.

Your failure to maintain comprehensive operational records may hinder the defense process and complicate the resolution of the liability demand.

We expect your organization to maintain standard commercial documentation practices consistent with your specific industry classification and operational scope.

F. If your lack of cooperation materially prejudices our ability to investigate or defend the action, we may formally deny the claim.

A determination of material prejudice is based on whether your actions or inactions significantly impaired the legal defense or increased the financial exposure.

We will issue formal written warnings if we determine that your level of cooperation is insufficient or detrimental to the ongoing investigation.

Continued non-compliance after the issuance of a formal warning will trigger a comprehensive review of your eligibility for ongoing liability protection.

The obligations detailed in this section apply equally to the primary named enterprise and any additional entities scheduled for protection.
